I have bought it many times in the past few days. The Chinese restaurant is on the second and third floors. It is very popular during the holidays, and there are many wedding banquets, so I ate there once because I couldn't decide on a location. The food is good, the portion is large, and the price is moderate and reasonable. Location: Opposite the Oujiang River, the scenery is good. Not far from Wuma Street in the city center, close to Jiangxin Island, there is also a Lingyue Plaza nearby, where you can find food and shopping. The location is very good, and it is very convenient if you don't want to eat in the hotel. You can also order takeout. I will definitely stay at Pullman Wenzhou again when I come to Wenzhou next time.
